<Operation>

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>POST</b></Pill> /rest/api/v1/addcollectionitems \{#operation-addcollectionitems\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_Add Collection item_

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Add items to a Collection.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

cURL

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent slot="content" id="operation-addcollectionitems+code-samples+curl">

<CodeSample>

```curl
curl https://{instance}-be.glean.com/rest/api/v1/addcollectionitems \
 -X POST \
 -H 'Authorization: Bearer YOUR_APITOKEN_HERE' \
 -d '{
  "collectionId": 87
}'
```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>POST</b></Pill> /rest/api/v1/createcollection \{#operation-createcollection\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_Create Collection_

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Create a publicly visible (empty) Collection of documents.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

cURL

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent slot="content" id="operation-createcollection+code-samples+curl">

<CodeSample>

```curl
curl https://{instance}-be.glean.com/rest/api/v1/createcollection \
 -X POST \
 -H 'Authorization: Bearer YOUR_APITOKEN_HERE' \
 -d '{
  "name": "ipsum eiusmod"
}'
```

</CodeSample>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### audienceFilters \{#operation-createcollection+request+audiencefilters\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

A list of filters for the query. An AND is assumed between different facetFilters. For example, owner Sumeet and type Spreadsheet shows documents that are by Sumeet AND are Spreadsheets.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<ExpandablePropertyBreakouts slot="breakouts">

  id="operation-createcollection+request+audiencefilters+facetfilter"

  hasExamples
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### groupName \{#operation-createcollection+request+audiencefilters+facetfilter+groupname\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Indicates the value of a facet, if any, that the given facet is grouped under. This is only used for nested facets, for example, fieldName could be owner and groupName would be Spreadsheet if showing all owners for spreadsheets as a nested facet.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<ExpandablePropertyExamples slot="examples">

_Example:_

```
Spreadsheet
```

</ExpandablePropertyExamples>

</ExpandableProperty>

<ExpandableProperty
  id="operation-createcollection+request+audiencefilters+facetfilter+values"

  parentId="audienceFilters_FacetFilter"

  typeAnnotations={`[]`}
  hasDescription
  hasEmbed
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### values \{#operation-createcollection+request+audiencefilters+facetfilter+values\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Within a single FacetFilter, the values are to be treated like an OR. For example, fieldName type with values [EQUALS Presentation, EQUALS Spreadsheet] means we want to show a document if it's a Presentation OR a Spreadsheet.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

  slot="tab"
  id="operation-editcollection+code-samples+curl"

>

cURL

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent slot="content" id="operation-editcollection+code-samples+curl">

<CodeSample>

```curl
curl https://{instance}-be.glean.com/rest/api/v1/editcollection \
 -X POST \
 -H 'Authorization: Bearer YOUR_APITOKEN_HERE' \
 -d '{
  "id": 87,
  "name": "ipsum eiusmod"
}'
```

</CodeSample>

  typeAnnotations={`[]`}
  expandByDefault
  hasDescription
  hasBreakouts
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### audienceFilters \{#operation-editcollection+request+audiencefilters\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

A list of filters for the query. An AND is assumed between different facetFilters. For example, owner Sumeet and type Spreadsheet shows documents that are by Sumeet AND are Spreadsheets.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<ExpandablePropertyBreakouts slot="breakouts">

<ExpandableBreakout
  id="operation-editcollection+request+audiencefilters+facetfilter"
  entryId="audienceFilters_FacetFilter"
  parentId="audienceFilters"

>

  hasExamples

  entryId="audienceFilters_FacetFilter_groupName"
  parentId="audienceFilters_FacetFilter"
  typeInfo={`{"label":"string","linkedLabel":"string","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}`}
  typeAnnotations={`[]`}
  hasDescription
  hasExamples
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### groupName \{#operation-editcollection+request+audiencefilters+facetfilter+groupname\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Indicates the value of a facet, if any, that the given facet is grouped under. This is only used for nested facets, for example, fieldName could be owner and groupName would be Spreadsheet if showing all owners for spreadsheets as a nested facet.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<ExpandablePropertyExamples slot="examples">

_Example:_

```
Spreadsheet
```

</ExpandablePropertyExamples>

</ExpandableProperty>

<ExpandableProperty
  id="operation-editcollection+request+audiencefilters+facetfilter+values"
  entryId="audienceFilters_FacetFilter_values"
  parentId="audienceFilters_FacetFilter"
  typeInfo={`{"label":"array","linkedLabel":"<a href=\\"#operation-editcollection+request+audiencefilters+facetfilter+values+facetfiltervalue\\">FacetFilterValue</a>","children":[{"label":"FacetFilterValue","linkedLabel":"<a href=\\"#operation-editcollection+request+audiencefilters+facetfilter+values+facetfiltervalue\\">FacetFilterValue</a>","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}`}
  typeAnnotations={`[]`}
  hasDescription
  hasEmbed
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### values \{#operation-editcollection+request+audiencefilters+facetfilter+values\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Within a single FacetFilter, the values are to be treated like an OR. For example, fieldName type with values [EQUALS Presentation, EQUALS Spreadsheet] means we want to show a document if it's a Presentation OR a Spreadsheet.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

  hasBreakouts

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### audienceFilters \{#operation-editcollection+responses+200+application-json+audiencefilters\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

A list of filters for the query. An AND is assumed between different facetFilters. For example, owner Sumeet and type Spreadsheet shows documents that are by Sumeet AND are Spreadsheets.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<ExpandablePropertyBreakouts slot="breakouts">

  hasExamples

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### groupName \{#operation-editcollection+responses+200+application-json+audiencefilters+facetfilter+groupname\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Indicates the value of a facet, if any, that the given facet is grouped under. This is only used for nested facets, for example, fieldName could be owner and groupName would be Spreadsheet if showing all owners for spreadsheets as a nested facet.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<ExpandablePropertyExamples slot="examples">

_Example:_

```
Spreadsheet
```

</ExpandablePropertyExamples>

</ExpandableProperty>

  id="operation-editcollection+responses+200+application-json+audiencefilters+facetfilter+values"

  typeAnnotations={`[]`}
  hasDescription
  hasEmbed
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### values \{#operation-editcollection+responses+200+application-json+audiencefilters+facetfilter+values\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Within a single FacetFilter, the values are to be treated like an OR. For example, fieldName type with values [EQUALS Presentation, EQUALS Spreadsheet] means we want to show a document if it's a Presentation OR a Spreadsheet.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<Operation>

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>POST</b></Pill> /rest/api/v1/editcollectionitem \{#operation-editcollectionitem\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_Update Collection item_

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Update the URL, Glean Document ID, description of an item within a Collection given its ID.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<OperationCodeSamplesSection slot="code-samples">

<CodeSampleTabbedSection>

<CodeSampleTab

```curl
curl https://{instance}-be.glean.com/rest/api/v1/editcollectionitem \
 -X POST \
 -H 'Authorization: Bearer YOUR_APITOKEN_HERE' \
 -d '{
  "collectionId": 87,
  "itemId": "ipsum eiusmod"
}'
```

</Operation>

<Operation>

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>POST</b></Pill> /rest/api/v1/getcollection \{#operation-getcollection\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_Read Collection_

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Read the details of a Collection given its ID. Does not fetch items in this Collection.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<OperationCodeSamplesSection slot="code-samples">

<CodeSampleTabbedSection>
